Shandong Province Improving Cotton and Silk Conditions 62

Extending Cotton Fields by 400,000 Mu

This Year's Harvest is Over 9,000 Dan

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong Provincial Construction Department is making considerable efforts to promote cotton and silk business at the end of the year. Last year, the department issued improved cotton seeds of Jinzi Cotton (East Shandong) and Duris Cotton (Northwest Shandong) to the cotton-suitable areas of Qidong, Gaoyuan, Boxing, Putai, Binxian, Huimin, Shanghe, Linyi, Deping, Xiajin, Gaotang, Linqing, Qiuxian, Guantao (Northwestern Shandong), Gaomi, Pingdu, and Changyi (Eastern Shandong). About 2 million catties have been sown and planted. It is estimated that this improved cotton seed will yield 100 catties of seed cotton per mu in the 17 counties this year, which can yield 30 catties of pure cotton, for a total of 40,000 dan of seed cotton, which can produce 120,000 dan of pure cotton. The Construction Department borrowed more than 1 million yuan from the bank to distribute to the cotton spinning cooperatives in various counties, and then lent to the cotton farmers to activate their economy. Instructors were sent to various counties to guide them to make their organization and management rationalized, and a cotton ginning and packing factory was established in Qidong to help its operation. If the weather and climate are normal this cotton season, and there are no special blows, the harvest will definitely be as expected in the budget. Calculated at a price of 40 yuan per dan, it can obtain more than 4.8 million yuan. In the past, the total cotton output in Shandong Province was only 1.8 million dan, worth more than 12 million yuan. The income from cotton spinning in the province this year has increased several times more than before. It is also heard that the Construction Department has a predetermined plan, and it can be extended to more than ten times next year. However, I am afraid that the bank will be suspicious of the loan due to the current situation, and there may be difficulties in not being able to maximize it. In the past, the silk-producing areas in Shandong Province, such as Linzi, Zhoucun, and Yidu, mostly transported machine-made silk overseas, earning about 4 million taels per year. The tussah silk in the coastal counties such as Fushan, Laiyang, Muping, and Qixia can also earn 1.5 million taels every year. Later, because overseas markets were gradually invaded, it suffered the same fate as Zhejiang silk. The Construction Department immediately devoted itself to the improvement of silkworm eggs and silkworm feeding, with Linqu as the center, and prepared to gradually promote it. A silk drying workshop was established in Linqu, a silkworm silk improvement center was established, and cooperatives were established. There has been a great improvement in recent years. Last year, 40,000 improved silkworm eggs were purchased from Zhejiang, and 1,000 eggs were distributed to Linqu and Qingzhou. Now it is the orchid flood season, and it is estimated that 9,400 dan of orchids can be harvested, worth 25 yuan per dan, for a total of 235,000 yuan. It is estimated that it will be expanded to 100,000 sheets next year, and the total income will be even more considerable. However, another silk drying stove must be added to meet the needs. In addition, the wheat in Jiaodong this year has been quite affected by "Dan disease", and the harvest is expected to be 60 to 70%. Many people are harvesting now.

Hunan Province's Attitude Toward Guangdong and Guangxi 63

He Jian sympathizes with resisting the enemy and saving the country, but insists on central leadership

Hankou Correspondence: Since Guangdong and Guangxi declared their intention to resist Japan and send troops to Tingzhou, the people of the whole country have been greatly shaken, and the three towns of Wuhan are especially concerned. This reporter recently learned that Liu Huarui, advisor to the Hunan Pacification Commissioner's Office and concurrently the provincial government, had arrived in Hankou. I specially visited him at Room 36 of the Deming Hotel in the French Concession. The following is a record of Mr. Liu's conversation: (Question) I heard that you and Director Zhu Jingnong came to Hankou from Changsha on official business. I came to inquire about the truth of Hunan Province's attitude toward the Southwest. (Answer) Director Zhu and I arrived in Hubei from Changsha by car a few days ago, but Director Zhu took a plane to Nanjing that day. The Hunan authorities' position on the situation remains the same as in the past. They insist that foreign affairs work must be done under the guidance of the overall national policy. Therefore, while they sympathize with resisting the enemy and saving the country, they must not be used by foreign enemies to control China, which is passive. (Question) It is rumored that you have an important mission this time to Hubei, and since you live in Hunan, you must have a plan in mind. I would like to know its main points. (Answer) When Guangdong and Guangxi first mobilized their troops, I had a discussion with Chairman He Yunqiao and immediately decided on a policy, believing that all provinces in the country should take the same action under the guidance of the overall national policy and not participate in civil wars. The next day, I conveyed this intention to all parties and published this view in various Hunan newspapers. As for this trip to Hubei, there is no special mission. (Question) I heard that you went to the Pacification Commissioner's Office stationed in Hubei, is that true? (Answer) Director He Xuezhu is an old acquaintance. A few days ago, I visited Director He at my convenience and exchanged views on the current situation. We shared the same opinion that the central government and the Southwest should do their best to resolve the national crisis peacefully, and it is especially important to recognize the difference between temporary anger and the overall national plan. (Question) Then, what will Hunan Province do to support the central government? (Answer) Hunan Province strives for the unity of the whole country and the revival of national culture, so as to create a solid central government with national consciousness, without mixing in the use of foreign forces to drive away the tiger from the front door and lead the wolf in from the back door. (Question) Does Tingzhou also have individual opinions to contribute to the central government? (Answer) Since Mr. He Yunqiao took charge of military and civilian affairs in Hunan Province, he has worked hard to propose to the central and local governments to treat each other with sincerity, and to seek to avoid any local struggles for power and private fights. Hunan Province is a strong shield for the central government. I hope that the central government will continue to pay attention to petty provocations in the future to avoid destroying the status quo in Hunan Province. (Question) According to your observation, this change is really due to Hunan Province's first advocacy of peace, and the central government and other provinces are all taking the overall national situation as a prerequisite to engage in peace movements. This is really a proof of the progress of Chinese people's wisdom in recent years. In the end, the whole country will inevitably return to unity. Bad soldiers are ominous, and everything will end with the overall national situation and what everyone wants. (13th)

Guangdong Province Decides to Divide into Six Zones for Air Defense Deployment 64

Air defense bonds to be issued on a regular basis

The Provincial Bank will advance funds to proceed

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangdong authorities have spared no effort in carrying out air defense deployment in recent years. Recently, in order to complete the provincial air defense plan as soon as possible, it was decided to implement the resolution of the Provincial Assembly to issue 10 million yuan of provincial people's air defense bonds. The issuance regulations have been drafted, and the first issuance period was originally scheduled to begin on the first day of this month. Later, due to the preparations not being complete, it was changed to the twentieth day of this month to officially issue. It is reported that after the issuance of the people's air defense bonds was decided, the provincial government, in order to ensure smooth progress and to show great impartiality, handed over the issuance work to the Provincial Assembly and asked them to prepare everything immediately so that they could be issued as scheduled. After the Provincial Assembly drafted the issuance regulations for the air defense bonds, it also actively carried out preparations, and now it is basically ready. However, in order to avoid difficulties and achieve twice the result with half the effort, it still sent the issuance work to the Department of Finance for handling and asked the department to order all county governments in the province to be responsible for assisting in the collection of bond funds to facilitate progress. The Department of Finance has agreed to follow suit and has sent personnel to take over. Recently, they are continuing to prepare and handle the unfinished procedures, and the official issuance was changed to the twentieth day of this month for this reason. The funds from these air defense bonds are designated for expanding air defense throughout the province, such as air defense equipment, construction of airfields, purchase of aircraft machinery, and all supplies. At present, the authorities have also decided to divide the entire province into East, South, West, North, Central, and Cliff six zones in the future to make a whole strict air defense deployment. After the bonds are officially issued, the Provincial Bank will first advance 5 million yuan to start implementation. When the second phase is issued, the bank will be asked to advance another 5 million yuan. The borrowed funds will be mortgaged with these 10 million yuan of air defense bonds, and they will be repaid in full after collection in the future.

Miscellaneous Writings on Rural Hubei 65

(Special Correspondent of this Newspaper, Cheng Jun)

17th: From Gucheng to Xiangyang

Returning to Gucheng from Shihua Street to wait for a car to return to Hekou and then to Xiangyang, it happened that the 40th Army was being transferred here. Armed comrades were constantly on the road, marching arduously, which was commendable. After waiting for a long time, a car arrived, fully loaded with sick soldiers from the army. Fortunately, I managed to squeeze on, but was eventually squeezed off. Between getting on and off, another topless car arrived, so I was able to climb on and travel again and again. The destination, Laohekou, was already in sight. The car stopped to cross the Xiang River. The 40th Army troops were gathering on the river beach, with a very neat military appearance. Entering the city was subject to strict inspection, which was very different from the situation when passing through here a few days ago. I was just unpacking at the inn when the army arrived and stationed in various rooms. The brigade commander was also stationed here. I called the waiter to prepare food, but the guards forbade me to speak because the officers were holding a meeting. I was not allowed to go downstairs either, so the freedom to eat, drink, and go to the toilet was deprived. Trapped in the encirclement, there was no rescue for a long time. I bravely went out to visit the brigade commander, but although I did not get to see him, I was fortunately allowed to go downstairs, but I was stopped again and not allowed to go up. I watched local officials and gentry coming and going. It was not until 12 o'clock in the evening that I was reported by the waiter and allowed to enter. Half of this day was spent in prison life and half in exile, all thanks to the army's transfer. Thinking of the four regiments with swords and halberds like a forest, I could not sleep all night.

I got up at dawn the next day and went straight to the station, as if escaping from a great disaster. On the way, I met a Mr. Someone I knew before, and only then did I know that a major incident almost happened here the day before. It turned out that the troops of the 40th Army were camping outside the city the night before. Soldiers from the Anti-Smoking Inspectorate's Anti-Smuggling Battalion went out of the city to inspect and, for some reason, a misunderstanding occurred, leading to a conflict. Several shots were fired, and one of the army's sentries was injured. Yesterday, the brigade commander came here, and the Guanghua County Government, the Hekou Chamber of Commerce, and Wu Tuanzhang of the 82nd Division and others tried their best to mediate and agreed on conditions, responsible for the injured, and if there were any accidents, they would be given considerable compensation, so the matter was settled. I asked where this money came from, and the answer was that it was borne by the local government. When a misunderstanding occurs in the military, both sides usually win. This is not the case today.

Traveling by car from Hekou, passing through the Taipingkou area, which was the area most severely affected by the flood last year, the road was surrounded by endless plains, all of which were fields covered with pressure, reaching tens of thousands of acres. Villages were completely shattered, and the scars could still be seen. When the flood first arrived, people climbed to the tops of trees to survive for three or four hundred, but without boats to rescue them, they could not withstand the hunger, cold, wind, and rain, and eventually fell into the flood and were buried in the belly of fish. In Taipingkou alone, thousands of farmers were drowned. The lives of our people are worthless, which is lamentable. Approaching Fancheng, heavy rain suddenly fell. The car I was riding in was open and there was nowhere to escape. My clothes were soaked. Pedestrians and travelers riding donkeys on the road were also in the wind and rain, driving and galloping, looking at each other as if they understood each other. Before long, the rain stopped and the car arrived at the station. Crossing the Han River to Xiangyang, it is customary to get out of the car when entering the city and pay respect to the soldiers guarding the city, with the feeling of "civil and military officials dismounting here." The soldiers seemed to be from the security regiment. It is said that if you don't get out of the car, the person sitting in the car will be insulted and the person pulling the car will be beaten severely. However, when paying respect to the soldiers, they sit on stools with their legs spread apart, their heroic demeanor awe-inspiring, and their arrogant attitude overflowing from their eyebrows. Although this is a small matter, it is very touching.

Xiangyang was formerly Xiangguo, located in the upper reaches of Jingchu, a hub between the north and the south, its danger is sufficient to consolidate, and its soil is sufficient for food. The Qing scholar Gu Zuyu said, "The situation in Huguang, in terms of the southeast, is important in Wuchang, in terms of Huguang, is important in Jingzhou, and in terms of the world, is important in Xiangyang." Although the situation has changed today, it still does not lose its important position. The county seat is located on the sunny side of the Han River, facing Fancheng, which has always been known for its commercial prosperity, across the river. Fancheng is an economic zone, while Xiangcheng is a military, political, and cultural zone, just like the confrontation in Wuhan. The Fifth District Commissioner's Office and the Second Branch of the High Court are located in the city, and there are countless other agencies and groups.

The number of schools is the highest in northern Hubei. In Xiangyang, there are Provincial Xiangyang High School, Provincial Junior High School, Provincial Rural Normal School, Provincial Elementary School, County Elementary School, and Hubei Northern Library and County People's Education Hall. In Fancheng, there are Private Xianbei High School, Shangzhi Elementary School, County Fancheng Elementary School, and Provincial Xiangyang People's Education Hall. Generally speaking, they are well managed, especially the Provincial High School and People's Education Hall. A student unrest occurred in the Provincial Junior High School the day before yesterday. The principal was beaten and left the school. The students went to the county party headquarters and the commissioner's office to petition, stating the principal's crimes and weeping. After the secretary of the commissioner's office persuaded them earnestly, they returned to school. For a time, there was a joke about "the principal bleeding, the students crying, and the secretary sweating." In addition, there are people's schools run by the county party headquarters and the Hubei Northern Zhongshan Daily, which can all work hard to promote culture, but due to the closed atmosphere and low level of people's intelligence, the effect is still small. The county was originally an area where humanities gathered, but now it is very different from the past, which is unexpected. When the reporter first arrived in Fancheng from Zaoyang, the car crossed a river and saw two fisherwomen scolding each other from different boats, spreading ugly voices everywhere for a long time, leaving a deep impression. After arriving in Fancheng, I got lost while visiting friends. I asked the citizens, who pointed me in random directions, and the police officers were the same, making me unable to adapt. I heard a friend say that they are slow-witted, not deliberately cunning. He gave an example, saying that when cars drive on the road, the villagers never avoid them. Even if the car honks its horn urgently, they still turn a deaf ear. Although the car can hurt people, they have not considered this at all. Later, what I saw on the road was indeed as he said. There are many prostitutes in Xiangyang City. It is not uncommon to see women laughing and playing in the streets. Last night, the commissioner's office checked residential buildings due to the alarm of an emergency in the territory and captured more than thirty pairs of illicit couples. It is not only that the people's intelligence is closed, but also that the atmosphere is deteriorating.

Scenic spots include Longzhong, Xianshou Xijia Pond, Lument Temple, Mi Gong Temple, Wang Can Building, Zhaoming Building, Zhang Jianzhi Temple, Du Gongbu Tomb, Wang Shuhe Tomb, etc. Only a fragment of stone remains of the Wang Building. The authenticity of the Du Tomb cannot be determined. There are many inscriptions in the Mi Temple, and his grandson is poor and addicted to smoking, selling rubbings to make a living. Longzhong is thirty miles west of the city, surrounded by mountains and forests, with Sangu Hall, Danbo Pavilion, Caolu Pavilion, Liangfu Rock, Yeyun Nunnery, Banyue Stream, Xiaohong Bridge, Genggengtian, Lotus Pond, Laolong Cave, Longwochu, and Eight-Corner Well. The drum pavilions of the Copper Drum Pavilion and other attractions are Xianshou is the first of Xianshan, four or five miles south of the city. A pavilion is built on it, and at the foot of the mountain is the Yang Du Temple, and the Dropping Tears Stele is in the temple. Xijia Pond is the residence of Xi Jian in the Jin Dynasty, with the beauty of pavilions, terraces, flowers, and trees. When Shan Jian was stationed in Xiangyang, he often got drunk here. There is spring water in the area, which is extremely clear and can irrigate the fields, so Xi Jian's reputation has become more prominent with his teeth. Lument Temple is in Fancheng, the hometown of Haoran, and is a must-see for tourists. Zhuge Gong's feather fan and turban, Yang Taichuan's light fur belt, Yan Wei's historical pen, and Meng Hao's poetic talent, the remaining charm of the flowing style, are magnificent between the Jiang and Han rivers. Now visiting its ruins is enough to evoke a sense of exploring the ancients, but there are Taoists in charge of all places, and with their vulgar customs, it is inevitable to spoil the scenery a little. (Sent from Xiangyang on May 20)

Songjiang 66

Major Robbery in Huangqiao Town

In Huangqiao Town, Songjiang, at about 1:00 AM on the 14th, more than a dozen robbers speaking local dialects suddenly arrived, holding fast guns, box cannons, flashlights, etc. Robbers with guns were stationed at each important intersection to keep watch. At the same time, they began to rob. As a result, the victims were Qing Xiasongzhai Fresh Meat Store, Tiandetang Pharmacy, Wu Zhengda Nanhuo Shop Fresh Meat Store, Chen Yuchang North and South Goods Store, Xu Songshou Pharmacy, and a beach boat belonging to Tang Yixiu was robbed, loaded with stolen goods and escaped towards Xietang. During the robbery, A Kuan, a helper at a certain teahouse, heard the noise and came out to see what was happening. He was injured in several places by the robbers with their gun butts. The principals are now checking the lost items to report the robbery.

Public Burial of Poet Zhu Yuanchu

The poet Zhu Yuanchu from Yun Jian was a diligent student in his youth. His poems and novels were published in various newspapers in Shanghai and were widely circulated for a time. He passed away in the tenth year of the Republic of China. In the same year, his wife, Ms. Xu Xian, committed suicide due to sorrow and family poverty, leaving behind a son and a daughter. The coffin was placed in a temple for sixteen years. Now, his close friends Yao Yuanchu and Li Zihan and others have raised funds to plan his burial. A public burial was held on the 14th in Yun Jian Cemetery. The ceremony was very grand, and Cai Zhongyu was recommended by all walks of life to preside over the sacrifice, and Ping Jinya, Li Zihan, Shen Shoukuang, and Tang Tiaojun assisted in the sacrifice. Then, relatives and friends helped the coffin to ascend to the tomb, and the funeral was completed. The local Rongbao newspaper specially published a special issue to accompany it. It is heard that Mr. Li and others are also properly planning for the orphans to help them become self-reliant, so as to comfort the deceased.

Wuxi 67

Construction in the 25th Year

The County Construction Bureau, at the beginning of the year, has specially included various important construction projects in the construction plan outline for the 25th year, and decided to hold a construction committee meeting at 2:00 PM on the 18th of this month to discuss various central tasks. At that time, the construction plan outline will be submitted for discussion and approval for implementation. In terms of water conservancy, it is planned to complete ten rivers this year, including Qintangjing, Luqu Bridge West River, Zhihu Bridge, Da Hong Bridge River, Heng River, Zhang Maoshe River, Wan Tang Bin, Yongxing River, South Zoumatang, and Yangshuyuan River, with an estimated cost of 8,540 yuan. The houses of the Shao and Gao families covered by the Liangxi River near Ximen and the riverside base will also be demolished to widen the river surface and allow the water source to flow smoothly, with an estimated cost of 3,318 yuan. In terms of building roads, the bridges, culverts, and road surface on the northern line of Hushan Road will be built to facilitate traffic around Wuli Lake and enhance the scenery of Hushan, with a total cost of 55,520 yuan. The Deyuan Road from Ximen Dexin Bridge to Kaiyuan Road has been filled with earthworks by labor service. The bridges, culverts, and road surface will then be completed, with an estimated cost of more than 13,400 yuan. The unrenovated section of Yangxi Road will also be renovated again so that the entire reconstruction can be completed, costing 1,114 yuan.

Resolution of Coarse Salt License

The sales of coarse salt in this county are limited, and a salt license is required to operate. Now the Salt Transport Deputy Envoy is sorting out the coarse salt licenses of various provinces and cities, and each license is stipulated to be 35 yuan. After obtaining the license, the sale of coarse salt can be operated. However, the license fee for refined salt is stipulated by the Ministry of Finance to be one yuan, so those who sell coarse salt believe that the burden is too heavy. They specially submitted a request to the Salt Transport Deputy Envoy to reduce the fee to be the same as that for refined salt. The Yangong Inn in this county received an approved instruction on the 13th, notifying the Liquor Hotel Industry Association to inform all members to go to the inn to receive the previously paid license fees.

Strike in Shierwei

More than 300 people, including representatives of the sail transport owners and salt boat workers of Shierwei and directors of the Yanpu Labor Union, came to Yangzhou to petition. After four days, the matter has not been resolved. Because the representatives petitioning in Yangzhou have not returned to the wei and there is no satisfactory news, all the laborers in Shierwei held a meeting at the Yanpu Labor Union on the 12th to plan to come to Yangzhou to participate in the petition. The person in charge of the Labor Union then returned to stop them, resulting in a conflict and the destruction of the Labor Union. The stores in Weishi also went on strike to express their support. It is heard that the salt workers had first petitioned the Yizheng County Government on the 13th, requesting the issuance of passports to come to Yangzhou to participate in the petition. The representatives of the shipping owners in Yangzhou heard the news and are now submitting it to the Salt Affairs Inspection Office and the Jiangdu County Party and government organs, requesting prompt relief to avoid expanding the situation.

Submitting to the Province to Explain the Housing Donation Rate

Jiangdu County Government, because it was ordered to collect housing donations, local people repeatedly submitted requests to the Provincial Department for exemption. However, the relevant notice was not approved. Now, the donation rate for self-produced shops and houses is based on one-thousandth of the property value of 1,000 yuan and 0.8 as the standard. Should those with a property value of less than 1,000 yuan be charged, and the regulations have no clear written regulations? On the 12th, the county government specially submitted a request to the Provincial Department for explanation.

Nantong 68

Water Police Seize River Pirates

The Jiangsu Provincial Water Police Team stationed in Tong seized river pirates Ling Gaosong, Liu Xuming, Xiao Wanyi, etc. on the Jiangmian of Baimao Port and transferred them to the Third District Department of Tongcheng. It was recognized that they had robbed the river surface and copied out many account books of the Xiechang Sheng Pig Shop.

Rape Case of a Female Teacher Sentenced

Three rickshaw drivers, Shao Quan and others, took turns raping a female passenger Wang Zilian, who was working as a female teacher. The case shook the entire county. The Criminal Court of Nantong Local Court sentenced Shao Quan and Ren Quan to eight years in prison on the 13th, Yan Heshang to seven years in prison, and Ren Zhao, who assisted in the rape, to three and a half years in prison.

Nanhui 69

Obstructing Injections Leads to Eye Gouging

Jin Rongsheng in Datuan Town, Eighth District, makes a living by privately selling morphine for people to inject. His nephew Baosheng repeatedly persuaded him not to listen. A few days ago, Shao Miaosheng, Jin Zugen, and Wu Qinsheng went to Rongsheng's house to inject morphine. Baosheng took the needles down and stopped them from injecting, which led to a grudge. Shao, Jin, and Wu dragged Baosheng out of the house at 11:00 PM on the 11th and used a small sharp knife to gouge out both of his eyes, rendering him disabled. Yesterday, Baosheng reported to the Second Substation of the town's Public Security Bureau, requesting detention and investigation. After the substation verified that it was true, it ordered the police to arrest the murderers and sent Baosheng to the county for examination of injuries.

Gaoyou 70

Department of Finance Recovers Old Taxes

The Department of Finance, in view of the fact that the arrears of taxes in various counties over the years are very large, stipulated last year that they should be paid in three installments. The first two installments have long been overdue. Although many counties have reported their payments, they are still far from the original arrears. Now that the deadline for the third installment is the end of June, the Department has specially ordered all counties to strictly pursue and report payments within the time limit. The county government received the Department's order on the 12th to strictly pursue the matter.

Liuhe 71

Violating the Law and Resisting the Use of New Weights and Measures

Sha Pengnian, the owner of the Sha Wanlong grain store in Nancheng outside the First District of this county (that is, Nancha Township), did not comply with the regulations on the use of new weights and measures, and still privately used the old weights and measures. After the inspectors found out, they reported to the county government, which ordered the public security section to send police to stop it. However, Sha resisted with strength and wickedness, and his neighbor Wang Mouru, who was in the same industry, helped him from the sidelines. The county government immediately sent many police officers to detain the owners of the Sha and Wang stores for interrogation. After the matter was proven, in addition to exempting them from the charge of obstructing official duties, they were punished for violating the law and resisting the use of new equipment, and each was fined seven yuan to serve as a warning.

Ningbo 72

Stagnation of Fritillary Cooperative

The Jinjiang Fritillary Cooperative has been plagued by internal disputes last year, and the cooperative affairs cannot proceed. In particular, the 　fritillary, which has already collected a fixed amount of money, cannot be received at full price, nor can the goods be sold. It is difficult to advance or retreat. At that time, Wang Shihe returned to his hometown on leave, and the members begged Wang to hold the method, and Wu Jing reluctantly agreed to come out and maintain it. The plan of operation has already 　has a clue. Recently, Wang realized that there are many internal disputes, and the 　is very deep. It is difficult to complete the rectification without giving full effort and sufficient time. It happened that he was ordered to cancel his leave, and he immediately resigned from the cooperative affairs. Therefore, the cooperative affairs fell into stagnation again. The loan from the Zhejiang Local Bank is now due, but no one is responsible in the cooperative, and the price of fritillary has plummeted. It is heard that it is planned to auction off more than a hundred jin of fritillary under mortgage to pay off the debt.

Taizhou 73

Discovery of Smuggled White Sugar

Recently, smuggled sugar has been discovered in Aohuan, Huangwan, Baibi and other townships in the Central District of Wenling, and the price is very cheap. It is heard that the smuggled goods are imported from Kanmen and Chumen on the coast of Yuhuan and transferred. The general ignorant people only know that the price is cheap, regardless of the outflow of money. The authorities have already investigated this matter.

Rice Plants Suffer from Insect Pests

Due to the cold and rainy weather this year, the rice plants in various townships in Wenling have not grown sufficiently, which makes farmers very worried. However, in Zeqian Shanglin, Danshui Bridge and other townships in the Northern District, insect pests have recently occurred. According to a farmer surnamed Wang, the insects are shaped like rice grains and are still in their infancy. If they are not quickly eradicated, they may spread widely.

Bandits Kill Squad Leader

On the morning of the 6th, at around 10:00 AM, Chen Zuolin, the head of the Zhuangding squad in Daxi Town, Northern District of Wenling, was secretly reported that more than 30 bandits were gathered in the Shigu Ridge area of Wanyu. The team leader immediately went to the area and found the bandits. The soldiers immediately opened fire and bombarded them for about an hour, killing one bandit, capturing one alive, and seizing a wooden-shell gun. The remaining bandits dispersed and fled. He led the troops back to defend. Passing by the front of Guanshan Elementary School, the bandits ambushed in the school and took the opportunity to open fire, killing squad leader Cai Boquan and a soldier. Seeing that their purpose had been achieved, the bandits fled. Team Leader Chen telegraphed the county government and sent Chen Zuomei to lead troops to suppress them.

Housing Problems in Peiping 74

Construction and Facilities

From the early Yuan Dynasty until the 16th year of the Republic of China, Peiping had always been the capital of our country. During this period, the nation's financial resources were concentrated here, and the city was managed and developed for six to seven hundred years. Today's grand scale is the result of the long-term efforts of our ancestors, which was no easy task. The architecture here tends towards bungalows; old-style multi-story buildings are rare, and Western-style buildings are mostly only two or three stories. Only hotel-style buildings like the Beijing Hotel and school-style buildings like the Red Building of Peking University have four or more stories. However, because they are all bungalows, they also occupy a lot of land. Currently, land is scarce in the entire city of Peiping, but one sees houses standing close together, with corners touching, all of which are dwellings. This kind of dense situation is the opposite of the city-and-forest, abundant land situation of Nanjing. Therefore, Nanjing, with a population of just under one million, already feels crowded, while this place, with a population of more than one and a half million, still feels spacious. The palace-style red walls, yellow tiles, upturned eaves, and flying corners of the architecture here have long been famous throughout the world as representatives of Eastern architectural art. Even ordinary buildings are mostly gray tiles and blue bricks, and the houses are all regularly square, both dignified and orderly. The two large doors are mostly painted red; green or black paint is also occasionally used. Copper or iron rings are installed on the doors for those who knock. Usually, electric bells are also installed above the door lintel, with both old and new side by side. The walls are thick, all over one foot four or five inches thick, and the roofs are also as thick as three or four feet, so they can block the wind and sun, and are warm in winter and cool in summer. Regardless of large or small households, all have spacious courtyards. The side rooms and main rooms are not connected, and the toilets and kitchens are also separated from the main house. Because of the sparse rainfall, grass does not grow in the courtyard, but flowers, trees, and vines are all planted to decorate it. More spacious ones also have gardens, in which towering trees sway in the wind.

The windows are mostly covered with two layers of gauze and white paper. However, this layer of white paper can be raised and lowered. It is raised when there is no wind and lowered when there is wind. In summer, those facing east and west have an additional layer of bamboo blinds. Inside the house, the doors are mostly single-leaf and mostly open outwards. Those going from inside to outside push the door, while those going from outside to inside pull the door. Those who are more particular also hang curtains on the doors in winter and summer, as this place is often windy and sandy, so this is necessary. Also, because of the climate, whether rich or poor, fire stoves must be lit indoors in winter. However, the rich have tall Western-style iron stoves, while the poor have short iron stoves. As for the installation of heating pipes, it is not common in private residences except in schools, hotels, and public institutions. This is due to both economic reasons and the architectural structure.

Levels of Housing

Schools and public institutions are generally in good condition. These cannot be considered as ordinary residences. Private residences can be roughly divided into three levels: upper, middle, and lower. Upper-class residences are mostly equipped with red-lacquered doors, electric lights, electric bells, telephones, and running water. Upon entering the gate, there is a guard room or reception room next to the gate, and a garage is attached for parking cars or rickshaws. The houses here usually have three courtyards, and some even have more than ten. The upper rooms, lower rooms, side rooms, study rooms, toilets, kitchens, and dining rooms and public living rooms are all available. Those with gardens naturally have flowers, plants, trees, and rocks. Even those without gardens have flowerbeds and shady trees in their courtyards. The value of each such residence is at least ten thousand yuan or more. Families living in such houses must have at least one guard and one rickshaw puller. Moreover, the expenses for electricity, water, and property taxes are no less than one hundred yuan per month. Middle-class residences are also quite impressive in appearance, but their structure is slightly simpler than that of upper-class residences. For example, upon entering the gate, there is usually no guard room, but a screen is erected to shield the interior of the house. In fact, after turning past the screen, there is only one or two courtyards of houses. The courtyard is generally not very large, and it is sometimes planted with flowers and plants, or slightly decorated with potted plants such as oleanders. The total number of rooms is about ten to twenty. Electric lights are naturally available in every household, but not many have their own telephone. Usually, several families share one, or they are called by a neighbor (called "street neighbor" here) who has a telephone and pay them one or two yuan per month for the electricity. Running water is usually available. If one has their own rickshaw, it can only be parked in the gatehouse or under a wide and deep corridor. The kitchen is usually only a half-shed, which only has a roof on one side and no ridge. The toilet is not a separate room, but is attached to the wall of the house, covered with a sheet of iron, and a deep pit dug below. The living room and study room are often in the same place. Although the structure of such residences is small, they are single-family and quite discreet and peaceful. It is most suitable for small families of two. The value of each is about one thousand to ten thousand yuan. If it is rented, the monthly rent is only about ten to twenty yuan.

The biggest feature of lower-class residences is that they are collectively inhabited; single-family residences are rare. The most typical representative of this type of residence is the "large courtyard." A large courtyard is surrounded by dozens or even hundreds of low houses. Each household lives in one or several low houses, but it is rare to have more than five rooms. The courtyard has no flowers or grass, only a muddy ground full of ash, soil, broken bricks, uneven. Rotting vegetables, rags, coal cinder, and accumulated soil are thrown in the shadows of the walls and the corners of the houses. When people pass by, flies buzz and fly. When the scorching sun shines, the foul odor is nauseating. The window openings are very small, and there is not enough light. Several members of the family often sleep on one kang (a heated brick bed). This kang has a very large area, with both ends against the wall, and its width occupies half of the entire room. Usually, cooking stoves are placed outside the door. When it rains, the stove is moved inside. At this time, although the factory doors are ventilated, it is unbearably hot. When it is hot, the courtyard is full of low tables, short stools, and broken mats. Men and women, old and young, sit and lie bare-chested among them. Sweat permeates the air, smelling like sour porridge. The people living in these large courtyards are mostly rickshaw puller families. There are 80,000 rickshaw pullers here, so large courtyards are everywhere. The monthly rent for each household is only a few dimes or one or two yuan.

Temporary Public Residences

Temporary public residences in Peiping can be roughly divided into five types: hotels, inns, hostels, apartments, and "chicken feather shops."

Hotels are mostly Western-style, with all modern facilities. Western food is available, and music can be listened to. Moreover, hotels such as the Beijing Hotel also have dance halls. Those who stay in these hotels are mostly wealthy officials or wealthy merchants. The daily room rate is at least two yuan or more. There are about eight or nine in total. The Beijing Hotel and the Six Nations Hotel are relatively luxurious. More economical ones, like the Beicheng Palace Hotel, cost only one yuan per day for the room.

Inns and hostels are slightly different here. The former began to flourish after the founding of the Republic of China, while the latter mostly has a history of several decades. The architecture and facilities of hostels are newer than those of inns. For example, the beds in hostels are copper beds, while those in inns are mostly wooden-framed spring beds. Moreover, hostels are mostly multi-story buildings, while inns are mostly bungalows. The management and service of hostels are also more advanced than those of inns. In terms of customers, hostels are mostly frequented by people from the academic and business sectors, while inns sometimes have customers from the countryside in addition to small merchants. Hostels are concentrated in the Xihua River area, such as the Jiaotong Hostel and the Zhengyang Hostel. Inns are concentrated in the Damochang and Luomashi areas, such as the Tianda Store and the Changfa Inn. In terms of room rates, hostels are more expensive than inns, with the former ranging from several dimes to several yuan, and the latter costing at most one yuan or more.

The number of apartments in Peiping is comparable to that of hotels, and they can be described as "standing in rows." This is because there are many schools here, but not many have dormitories. On the other hand, there are many vacant houses available for rent. The custom of Peiping people making a living by renting out rooms has a long history. To meet the needs of society, renting out their houses has become a trend. The houses and facilities of apartments are equivalent to middle-class residences. Most of the residents are students. The monthly rent for a room is about three to five yuan. If meals are included, it costs about twelve to fifteen yuan.

"Chicken feather shops" are temporary lodgings for beggars, vagrants, street performers, and petty thieves. It only costs five or six coppers per person per night (about three large copper coins). These chicken feather shops are mostly located in the Tianqiao area. The shops are covered with piles of chicken feathers, on which the lodgers can sleep at will. The suffering here is like one being in heaven and the other in hell, compared to those living in Western-style buildings with spring beds and silk quilts.

Page 10

City News: President Jiang Replies to Major Universities in the City

Central News Agency reports: Fourteen university presidents in this city, including Weng Zhilong, concerned about the mobilization of Guangdong-Guangxi troops invading Hunan, sent a telegram to the Guangdong-Guangxi authorities on the 11th, urging them to pull back, and telegraphed the central government, asking for sincerity to eliminate the hidden divisions in the nation. After receiving the telegram, President Jiang replied on the 13th. Rumor of Guangdong Freezing Legal Tender, Banking Circles Believe It Difficult to Implement 80

Financial Panic and Sealing Will Be More Unfavorable

Exchange Rate of Shanghai-Guangdong Silver Yuan Has Not Risen

New News Agency reports: According to a Reuter's dispatch from Guangzhou, the Guangdong authorities are preparing to freeze banknotes in Guangzhou banks and suspend withdrawals in order to curb the sharp decline of Guangdong currency. However, according to inquiries by a reporter from the New News Agency, banking circles in this city have not received any relevant news. They only know that after the tense situation, the value of Guangdong currency has fallen, and the demand for central legal tender is high, resulting in tight credit. If it is suddenly frozen, Guangdong's finances will become more panicked. Since the currency reform, a management committee for legal tender reserves has been established in Guangzhou to handle legal tender matters, all of which are presided over by the committee. It is expected that this matter will be difficult to implement. In addition, the exchange rate of Shanghai-Guangdong silver yuan is still around 640 yuan and has not shown an upward trend. However, in order to stabilize public sentiment, in addition to legitimate commercial remittances, ordinary remittances are restricted.

Complete Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bonds

Chinese and Foreigners Enthusiastically Subscribe

Allocate by Proportion Due to Oversubscription

Zhakou Cao'e River Section to be Put Out to Tender and Construction to Commence Soon

After the issuance of £1.1 million of 6% British gold bonds for the completion of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and HSBC acted as agents for the subscription. Chinese and foreigners applied very enthusiastically. It is expected that the subscription will be fully closed before the 17th. In particular, British people subscribed the most, because our country's bonds have a good reputation in the London market, and the prices have soared. Foreigners are happy to buy them. For example, the British gold bonds issued before were also subscribed through the above four banks. As a result, the subscriptions exceeded the total amount of the bonds. It was unavoidable to allocate them proportionally. Therefore, if the subscriptions for this bond exceed the total amount, the proportional allocation will be handled as before. Now that the Ministry of Railways has issued the bonds, in addition to the Qiantang River Bridge, which is under active construction, the section from Zhakou to Cao'e River of the incomplete Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway has been surveyed long ago and will soon be put out to tender for construction.

The 15th Municipal Health Campaign Opens This Morning at the People's Education Center 90

Sharp Decline in Yangtze River Shipping 91

Six Companies Resolve to Reduce Schedules and Suspend Ships

Chinese and foreign shipping merchants regard the Yangtze River route as the lifeblood of their business. Since the six companies formed an alliance last year to share the profits, water fees have been increased, rebates have been reduced, and the size and weight measurements have all been made less lenient. In addition, the Pingzhun Yanghang was commissioned to handle the measuring and weighing, etc. As a result, the cargo of guest families has been changed to be transported by private boats, trains, and parcel post. Therefore, the six companies have suffered a major blow in their business. Recently, due to various environmental reasons, the volume of cargo transportation on the Yangtze River has formed a rare sharp decline in decades. Now, there is a phenomenon of overcapacity and shared losses. For this reason, the six companies have held repeated plenary meetings to discuss remedial measures. The consensus is to reduce schedules, suspend ships, investigate the actual situation, and then determine fundamental policies. Details are as follows:

Business Losses

The section from Shanghai to Hankou is called the "Yangtze River Money," and the section from Hankou to Yichang is called the "Mid-Yangtze River Money." The ships of the six companies sailing on these two routes calculate the cargo load according to the profit-sharing system. The results were good in the second half of last year. This year, from January to the present, for half a year, both inbound and outbound cargoes have declined month by month. Since the implementation of measurement, it has plummeted. Since April, there have been very few goods transported from Shanghai's main street to the Yangtze River. Comparing this year's cargo volume with the same period last year, some are 60% of what it was, and some are only half. Although there are more than one reason, the water fee income of each company has suffered too much loss.

Maintain Profit Sharing

Yu Feipeng, the acting Minister of Transportation, came to Shanghai for this matter and summoned the responsible representatives of China Merchants, Sanbei, Ningshao, and other shipping companies to discuss relief measures. At that time, he advocated improving the profit-sharing system, but after consultation, it was believed that if the alliance agreement were abolished, it would inevitably lead to an oversupply of price competition and depreciation of water fees. As a result of the consultation, the original profit-sharing system was maintained. However, the issue of leniency for measured goods was negotiated to find a compromise solution to appease guest families. At the same time, Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and Nissin were informed of this intention. Therefore, the profit-sharing agreement is still maintained as usual.

Reduce Schedules and Suspend Ships

The Yangtze River liners of the six companies are 13 ships from Taikoo, 10 ships from Jardine Matheson, 7 ships each from China Merchants and Sanbei, 7 ships from Nissin, and 2 ships from Ningshao (including the Mid-Yangtze River ships, the six companies have a total of 68 ships in the profit-sharing agreement). Recently, the upstream and downstream Yangtze River ships of each company have only 30-40% of their capacity, and the freight revenue is not enough to burn coal. Therefore, the six companies held a meeting to discuss this issue last Wednesday. According to this business, it is difficult to maintain. Unless the six companies collectively reduce schedules and suspend ships, there is no way to save it. It was unanimously decided on the spot that Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, China Merchants, Sanbei, and Nissin, etc., each have no more than four Yangtze River schedules per week (including the Shanghai direct to Yichang ship and the direct to Xiangtan ship). According to the current number of ship schedules, at least six schedules will be reduced each week, and 24 ships must be reduced each month.

Not Yet Consistent

The British-owned Taikoo Company has already taken the lead in reducing Yangtze River ships. The company used to have a direct Shanghai to Yichang liner, which was guaranteed to sail once a week. Now it has begun to suspend flights and has reassigned the Changsha ship in the Yangtze River to the Hankou Yichang schedule and will no longer come to Shanghai. In the above proposal to reduce schedules and suspend ships, the representatives of the six companies stated that the losses of the ships whose schedules are suspended and cancelled by each company will still be compensated by the profit-sharing fund to show fairness. However, Nissin Company opposed it, on the grounds that each time the company's Yangtze River ship sails, the government pays a subsidy, and the Shanghai company has no right to reduce schedules. Therefore, the six companies still need to discuss the Nissin issue.

Send Personnel to Investigate

The six companies believe that the sharp decline in Yangtze River business in the past two months this year, the real reason for which cannot be understood without going to the Yangtze River for a whole inspection and investigation. In order to facilitate timely discussion of remedial measures, it has been jointly discussed and decided to organize a six-company group Yangtze River Investigation Committee. It has been decided to appoint the Taikoo Taipan, the Jardine Matheson Taipan, Zeng Guangqing, the business section chief of China Merchants Bureau, Wu Delin, the deputy manager of Sanbei, and Lu Yuyang, the director of Ningshao. They will depart from Shanghai at the end of this month, and each port along the Yangtze River must be thoroughly investigated to serve as the basis for remedial measures.

Qiu Jiang Wharf to Hold Groundbreaking Ceremony Regularly 92

To be Held at 3:00 PM on the 20th

The Central Bank's Qiu Jiang Wharf has been under construction for a year now. Each project has a considerable scale. It is scheduled to lay the cornerstone at 3:00 PM on the 20th of this month and hold a grand groundbreaking ceremony. Invitations are sent to Chinese and foreign people from all walks of life to participate. The recent construction situation of the wharf is recorded as follows:

Wharf Traffic Construction Completed

The only access road to Qiu Jiang Wharf is Wuquan Road. The road section from the wharf to Jungong Road was stipulated by the municipal government long ago, but the municipal government's funds were insufficient and it has not been built. The Qiu Jiang Wharf will soon be completed. If the road section is not built, the wharf's traffic will be inconvenient. Therefore, the Central Bank cooperated with the municipal government. The Central Bank allocated 150,000 yuan for road construction at one time, half of which was used as a loan from the municipal government and half of which was borne by the Central Bank. The road project was tendered and constructed by the Municipal Bureau of Public Works. The construction has been going on for several months and is being rushed. It will soon be completed. After the road is completed, those who go to the wharf no longer need to take a ferry from Dinghai Island. They can reach Jungong Road from Yangshupu, turn into Wuquan Road, and go directly to the wharf.

Set Up a Railway to Connect with the Songhu Line

In order to facilitate the combined transportation of water and land, the Qiu Jiang Wharf plans to lay several railway lines before and after the wharf, which will merge into one at Wuquan Road and connect to the Songhu Line along the northern part of the city center, about nine kilometers long. The Two Roads Administration has planned this railway, which requires more than 700,000 yuan. How to raise this cost is currently being discussed by the Central Trust Bureau and the Two Roads Administration. In the future, the construction of this route will greatly facilitate the transportation of passengers and goods, which is truly a characteristic of the Qiu Jiang Wharf.

Timber Piles Arrive Late, Affecting the Project

The timber piles needed for huge buildings in our country all come from overseas. The Qiu Jiang Wharf project is huge, so it is no exception. About thousands of timber piles are needed, all of which are 100 feet or 120 feet long, ordered from the United States by the contractor, Chuangxin Construction Company, and shipped to Shanghai in succession. It was originally scheduled to arrive in March of this year. Recently, there was a strike at the American timber pile company, resulting in hundreds of timber piles not being delivered. The wharf warehouse project was originally scheduled to be completed in 90 days, so it will be slightly affected. The completion date may be slightly delayed. The Qiu Jiang Wharf is our country's only large wharf. The equipment must be perfect. Various machines, such as cranes and cargo trolleys, are being purchased from various foreign merchants for installation and use at the wharf.

Preparing for the Groundbreaking Ceremony

The Central Bank's Qiu Jiang Wharf has been under construction for a year now. Each project has a considerable scale. Now the bank is scheduled to lay the cornerstone at 3:00 PM on the 20th of this month and hold a grand groundbreaking ceremony. Invitations have been sent to people from all walks of life, and hundreds of invitation cards have been sent out. The bank's President Kong Yongzhi and the Chairman of the Qiu Jiang Wharf Construction Committee, Song Ziliang, and all the committee members will all go to give speeches at that time. This groundbreaking ceremony was started by the Qiu Jiang Wharf Affairs Office of the bank a month ago. The General Affairs Section is responsible for preparing the layout of the ceremony site and the ships for picking up and dropping off guests. The reception will be handled by all senior staff of the Trust Bureau. The publicity will be handled by Zhu Shikang, the Deputy Manager of the Trust Bureau, and Xu Lisheng, the Secretary.

Central Bank Publishes Commemorative Album

The Central Bank will also publish a commemorative album and distribute it to all guests for commemoration and publicity. There are many comments from managers of major foreign shipping companies on the commemorative album, as well as an introduction by Minister Kong, the plan of Song Ziliang, chairman of the Qiu Jiang Wharf Construction Committee, to build the Qiu Jiang Wharf, and many papers by Mayor Wu and Guo, the Director of the International Trade Bureau. It can be seen that this groundbreaking ceremony of the Qiu Jiang Wharf is of great significance. Here is a copy of the program list of the groundbreaking ceremony: Chairman Song Ziliang of the Qiu Jiang Wharf Construction Committee delivers the opening speech, Minister Kong delivers the address, Mayor Wu delivers the address, the Public Security Bureau plays music, Minister Kong performs the groundbreaking ceremony, photography, tea party.

Special Steamer to Welcome Guests

Those who go to watch the ceremony that day can take a car to the bottom of Dinghai Island in the fish market and take a special steamer provided by the Central Trust Bureau to the Qiu Jiang Wharf. A detailed route map is printed on the back of the invitation card for guests to refer to in detail. Because the road from Jungong Road to the wharf is currently under construction and has not yet been completed, those who go to the Qiu Jiang Wharf can take a car directly when it is completed soon without having to take a ferry from Dinghai Island.

Dyeing and Weaving Association Submits a Petition to Control the Import of Cotton Cloth 93

Strict Industrial and Commercial Organization

The Machine Dyeing and Weaving Industry Association of this city, based on the resolution of the 7th Members' Congress, submitted a petition to the government to control the import of cotton cloth and strictly organize the association. Letters were submitted to the Ministry of Industry and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for handling. Details are as follows:

Petition to the Ministry of Industry

The petition is for the matter of petitioning to control the import of cotton cloth. It is believed that the scourge of smuggling is enough to endanger the foundation of the country. Only in special areas, under the trampling of foreign forces, efforts are made to prevent it, but it cannot be achieved in the end. The members of the association are based on the sincerity of saving the country and themselves, and they are all anxious day and night. Therefore, they believe that controlling trade is a targeted medicine to prevent smuggling. Cotton cloth is an item that our country already has a large amount of production and has reliable statistics, so it is possible to implement it first. Therefore, it was proposed and resolved by the 7th Members' Congress to petition the government to establish a cotton cloth import control agency, which will approve import credentials for the number of items that our country produces the least, and then import them from foreign countries for merchants to sell. Since imports are restricted, smuggling is easy to prevent. The matter is hereby presented to your ministry for verification and handling.

Letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

It is found that the current laws and regulations of the Industry Association lack detailed regulations on the sanctions against non-member colleagues, so that the organizations of each industry association are loose and cannot exert a powerful function. At this moment, the government has entrusted the Industry Association with the power to report smuggling and assist in investigation. It is deeply felt that the responsibility is heavy, and it is necessary to petition the government to amend the laws and regulations of the Industry Association as soon as possible, so as to strictly organize the organization. When the 7th Members' Congress of our association discussed this case, all members agreed that it was specially based on the case and sent to your association for investigation, and begged to be allowed to forward it to the government's competent authorities for speedy amendment of the laws and regulations of the Industry Association, and to include the articles that force colleagues to join the association.

Zhejiang Sericulture Control Committee: Silk Cocoon Testing Completed, Cocoon Released 95

Those Who Do Not Conform Must Pay a Deposit; Cocoon Shops Stop Weighing, Silk Factories Start Work One After Another

The Zhejiang Sericulture Control Committee detained those who bought cocoons at prices below the standard price from silk merchants and remnant cocoon merchants. Now the spinning and conversion test has been completed, and the detained cocoons have been completely released. The silk factories have started work one after another. Details are as follows:

Spinning and Conversion Test Completed, Detained Cocoon Released

After the Shanghai Silk Factory Industry Association telegraphed the Zhejiang Sericulture Control Committee to quickly release the detained spring cocoons, the control committee immediately sampled and tested the spinning and conversion, which has now been completed. This year, the quality of ten kinds of cocoons in Haining Chongde and other places is inferior to last year, with about 600 catties of fresh cocoons per market dan of silk, while the original standard was 550 catties of fresh cocoons per dan of silk. Therefore, the detained cocoons have been completely released. However, those whose spinning and conversion are the same as the original standard, but the purchase price is below the standard number, will also be released, but a deposit must be paid, about one yuan per dan, depending on the level of the purchase price, and then the punishment method will be determined.

Collect Improvement Fee of 6 Jiao Per Dan

The control committee collects a silkworm improvement fee, which is set at 6 jiao of national currency per dan of dried cocoons. 290 catties of fresh cocoons are combined into one dan of dried cocoons. When the cocoon merchants who collect the cocoons dry and ship them, they must be verified by the control committee, and the reported number of cocoons collected must be consistent. For example, if 290 dan of fresh cocoons are collected, 100 dan of dried cocoons should be baked according to the regulations. If the baking and conversion are slightly tender, those who bake 100 dan of dried cocoons must make up for the improvement fee of 10 dan of dried cocoons.

Cocoon Shops Stop Weighing, Silk Factories Start Work

Since the Zhejiang Control Committee cracked down on cocoon merchants raising and lowering cocoon prices, silk factories and remnant cocoon merchants have purchased at standard prices, that is, 21 yuan for native cocoons and 30 yuan for improved cocoons. Now, the cocoon shops that buy native cocoons in Zhejiang have stopped weighing one after another. The cocoon shops that buy improved cocoons and the cocoon shops that buy improved cocoons in Jiangsu will also stop weighing. The quality of cocoons is better than that of Zhejiang Province, and the silk factories in Wuxi, Zhejiang, Shanghai, and other places have started spinning silk one after another. As far as Shanghai is concerned, there are more than 20 companies in total, such as Hengcang.

Minfeng Paper Mill Hosts Visitors from All Sectors in Jiaxing 99

The entire plant's engineering equipment is extremely grand and precise. The factory also holds its sixth shareholders' meeting.

Huashang Minfeng Paper Company held its sixth shareholders' meeting in Jiaxing yesterday and invited people from all walks of life to visit the factory's facilities in Jiaxing, as well as to tour South Lake, returning in the evening. The details are as follows:

Attendees: Many people from all walks of life were invited yesterday, including prominent figures from industry, commerce, journalism, and representatives from government agencies. Those who attended included Xu Fu, Director of the Municipal Finance Bureau; Wu Huanru, Section Chief of the Social Affairs Bureau; Chu Huiseng, President of Shanghai Law School; Jin Runxiang and Yan E’sheng from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Huang Yanfang, Executive Director of the Shanghai Fish Market; Lao Jingxiu from Nanyang Company; Sun Meitang from the Ningbo Native Place Association; Xu Maotang from Zhonghui Bank; Zhou Xuexiang and Shao Xubai from the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions; Yan Duh He from the Xinwen Bao; and reporters from various news agencies. The company’s entire board of directors, including Yu Zuoting, Jin Tingsun, Xie Heng, Zhang Jiguang, General Manager Zhu Meixian, and all employees, totaling over 500 people, were warmly received by General Manager Zhu and other staff.

Arrival in Jiaxing: Participants arrived at the North Station before 8:35 AM yesterday, boarding a special train chartered by the company. The train departed at 8:35 AM and arrived at 10:40 AM with few stops along the way. Attendees then proceeded to the company's conference hall and rested on the lawn. When the train arrived at the station, company personnel were already there to greet them, and students from Minfeng Elementary School welcomed them on-site. Welcome flags and posters were displayed along the route, providing a very thoughtful reception.

Welcome Arrangement: The company's planned welcome arrangement for guests and shareholders was as follows: Guests and shareholders gather in the garden; Raise the national and factory flags, with cannon salutes; Elementary school students sing a welcome song; Photography; Opening of the welcome meeting; Tour; Guests tour South Lake; Shareholders' Meeting.

Welcome Speech: Chairman Xu Fu gave a welcome speech to the guests, saying: Today is the day of the sixth shareholders' meeting of the Minfeng Paper Mill. We are extremely pleased and honored to have so many distinguished guests from all walks of life in attendance. In recent years, due to my heavy involvement in government affairs, General Manager Zhu Meixian has been primarily responsible for the factory's affairs, for which I feel greatly indebted. The factory has been in operation for seven years, and its management and operation have been excellent. During these seven years, the entire society has been in a state of economic recession, with factories and industrial organizations closing down and failing one after another. However, our factory has been able to continue to move forward as usual, which is truly due to the efforts of the assistant managers. I still remember that President Chiang Kai-shek stated in his New Year's Day broadcast speech this year that productive construction is an essential plan for saving the country. We can increase production by establishing factories, solve the livelihood of many people, block leaks, and increase tax revenue, which is of no small benefit to the country and society. If all factories in the country could develop like our factory, then we would surely become strong. Today, those present are well-known figures from industry, commerce, and journalism. I hope that the journalistic community will promote and guide us, and that the financial and commercial communities will provide support and assistance so that our factory can progress day by day.

Establishment Process: After Mr. Xu's speech, General Manager Zhu Meixian proceeded to report on the establishment process of the factory, saying: Our factory was founded in 1930. In 1930, there were six paper mills in the country, one of which was named Hefeng. All six factories have since failed, due to their inability to compete with a certain national organized factory. Each factory had an annual production of over 3,000 tons, while China only needed 2,000 tons, which led to price wars. For example, the original selling price of kraft paper was 80 taels of silver per ton, but it fell to 20 taels. Our factory then purchased the Hefeng factory, which caused great pain at the time. We then tried to improve and unite with other factories in the same industry to establish a joint business office to reduce unnecessary competition. However, there is still one paper mill that has not joined, which is still a drawback. After that, prices gradually recovered, but production was still high, and the surplus was all kraft paper, while the paper needed for other purposes was still not produced and was all imported. For example, the stiff paper inside cigarette tubes has annual sales of 10,000 to 20,000 tons, and the jacquard paper boards used for printing in silk weaving factories, as well as other papers, are all foreign goods. Therefore, our factory is unwilling to produce kraft paper with other factories in the same industry, and the Hangzhou Huafeng factory, a sister factory, has also stopped production at the same time. In this way, only four factories are producing kraft paper, and supply and demand may be equal. Our factory, on the other hand, specializes in the production of jacquard paper and paper used for cigarettes, especially with a large amount purchased by the domestic Nanyang Tobacco Company. Last year, our factory reallocated 750,000 in capital to produce cigarette paper (i.e., the paper outside the cigarette). Although it has not yet reached a state of complete success, it is already applicable. The Nanyang Tobacco Company and four or five other Chinese tobacco factories have already placed orders. We hope for assistance from all parties in the future.

Speeches by Representatives: Subsequently, shareholder representative Chu Huiseng gave a speech, saying: I am a representative of the shareholders of both the current Minfeng and the former Hefeng factory. When Hefeng was founded in 1925, there was only one paper mill in the country, so supply and demand were in line, and it was possible to profit. Later, many others followed, and with the dumping of Japanese goods, as well as the Qi-Lu War, Hefeng completely failed and went bankrupt. Fortunately, at this time, we were able to have Mr. Mei and other new shareholders continue to operate. Although Hefeng is now a thing of the past, the factory's foundation still exists. The development of a business depends on its own efforts, but it also depends on the support and assistance of all sectors. However, the development of domestic goods also depends on tariff protection, so that foreign kraft paper can also disappear. Currently, due to smuggling, smuggled paper can enter without tax, which is a crisis for our factory and other factories in the same industry. I hope that all guests will work with our factory to resist smuggled goods, which would not only be fortunate for our factory, but also for all domestic goods factories. After Mr. Chu's speech, Mr. Yan Duh He, a reporter from the Xinwen Bao, gave a speech, saying that in the past, there were two reasons for the failure of domestic goods: after losses, there were no successors to continue the struggle; domestic goods manufacturers would attack and envy each other. The Minfeng factory was able to actively operate after the failure of its predecessor and propose to form a joint venture with various factories. This is how it can consolidate its commercial war front and succeed. It is not a fluke. Today, it has invented domestic cigarette paper, allowing us to smoke pure domestic cigarettes, and its spirit is truly admirable. Subsequently, Mr. Wu Huanru, Section Chief of the Social Affairs Bureau, and Mr. Ling Ruigong, a representative of the Zhejiang Construction Department, delivered congratulatory speeches (details omitted). After the speeches, lunch was held in the hall. After the meal, the guests were accompanied by the factory's staff to visit the entire plant and to tour South Lake. The shareholders' meeting was held in the evening.

Engineering Overview: The Minfeng Paper Mill is located near the East Railway Station in Jiaxing, at the former site of the Hefeng Paper Mill. It was founded in 1930 with a capital of 1.25 million. The chairman is Xu Fu, and the general manager is Zhu Meixian, assisted by Jin Runxiang. The factory covers an estimated area of over 100 acres and is a large-scale paper mill in the country. Its main projects are as follows: Steel Rolling Workshop: The raw materials for the cigarette paper produced by the factory are waste hemp and broken fishing nets. Therefore, a steel rolling workshop is set up to roll the fishing nets into small pieces, which can then be used to extract fiber. Ash Removal Workshop: The raw materials such as hemp cloth are cleaned of ash and soil. Material Selection Workshop: The raw materials are selected and cut into small pieces to prepare for pulping. The female workers in the workshop wear gas masks to prevent impurities from entering their mouths. When reporters visited, they saw that the female workers were practicing military exercises. Pulping Workshop: After the raw materials are sorted, they are sent to the pulping workshop. The workshop is equipped with various pulping machines, which are used to grind the materials into a liquid pulp. The initial pulp is not clean. After refining by several machines, it becomes a pure white pulp. Paper Making Room: The clean pulp is added to the machine, rolled. Before long, a clean, white sheet of paper is made, which is rolled out by the machine. At this point, the papermaking process is complete. The strength of the paper is tested by machine to determine its quality. In addition to the engineering facilities, the factory also has a school for the children of workers (Minfeng Elementary School) and a after-hours school for supplementary education. It can be called a prototype of a model factory in our country.

Car Drives Into Creek at No. 33 on Border of Chinese and International Concessions 101

None of the three people in the car were injured. Zhu Sichun was injured and sent to the hospital.

Fan Shaoceng, former commander of the First Division of the Sichuan Army of the Twenty-First Army, has resided in Shanghai for a long time and owns a private car. The registration number is 33 in both the Chinese and International Concessions. Yesterday, a friend of Fan surnamed Wang borrowed the car from Fan and went to the Zhapu seaside for fun with three friends and a bodyguard. On the way back, it was already half past four in the afternoon. When driving through Beiqiao in Shanghai County, another car was driving slowly in front. Fan's chauffeur, impatient for a moment, accelerated to overtake the car. Accidentally, Fan's car plunged into the creek, and the car overturned. None of the three people in the car were injured. However, Zhu Sichun (56 years old), a farmer living in Sanbao, Jingtuxiang, Shanghai County, happened to be passing by and was injured in the head and waist. The branch of the County Public Security Bureau heard the news and sent police to the scene. First, the injured person was sent to Beiqiao Hospital for dressing, and then transferred to Shanghai Hospital. The car was then recovered from the creek and sent to Shanghai for repairs.

Zhang Derong Accidentally Shoots Himself and Others While Cleaning Gun 102

Zhang injured in three places on his hands and feet. Two neighboring girls may be disabled.

Velvet merchant Feng Zhijie resides at No. 6 Shouxiang Lane, Fangbang Bridge, Minguo Road. Feng joined the Sixth Team of the South Shanghai Defense Corps as a volunteer member last year. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, Zhang Derong, the squad leader of the same Defense Corps team, who lives at No. 250 Fangxie Road, and team member Gu Hong, both armed, were waiting in front of Feng's house. Thinking it was still early, Zhang was cleaning his handgun when it suddenly went off accidentally. In a panic, he threw it on the ground. Unexpectedly, the gun fired four bullets in quick succession, injuring Zhang in three places on his left hand, left foot, and right foot. Stray bullets hit Zhao Huilian (6 years old), a girl living next door at No. 8, in the left leg, and Chen Baodi (12 years old, from Ningbo), a girl living across the street at No. 2, in the left kneecap. Fellow team members Gu Hong and Feng Zhijie, as well as beat police, rushed to send the injured to Qu Zhifu Hospital for treatment. The squad leader's injuries were serious, while the two girls were less critical. Chen Baodi's knee joint was injured and may be disabled. The Ximen Branch Director's police went to the scene of the incident, as well as the Defense Corps headquarters, to investigate the incident and reported it to the General Bureau for review. The handgun's serial number is 5444, which belongs to Gu Hong and was lent to squad leader Zhang Derong. It has now been taken into custody by the team headquarters.
